async (req, res) => {\\n    try {\\n        const { user_type, raw_transcript, page_route } = req.body;\\n        console.log(`[LOG] ${user_type}: \\\"${raw_transcript}\\\"`);\\n        \\n        const lower = (raw_transcript || '').toLowerCase();\\n        const sentiment = lower.match(/\\\\?/) ? 'curiosity' : (lower.match(/good|great|thank/) ? 'positive' : 'neutral');\\n        const intent = lower.match(/show|open|go/) ? 'navigation' : 'general';\\n        \\n        // Insert ledger\\n        const ledger = await pool.query(\\n            `INSERT INTO global_interaction_ledger (user_type, raw_transcript, page_route, sentiment, intent]\\n        );\\n        \\n        // Boss input\\n        if (user_type === 'boss') {\\n            await pool.query(`INSERT INTO boss_voice_inputs (raw_text, processed, priority) VALUES ($1, false, 'high')`, [raw_transcript]);\\n        }\\n        \\n        // Feed\\n        await pool.query(\\n            `INSERT INTO realtime_feed (feed_type, title, description, user_type, icon, page_context)\\n             VALUES ('voice', $1, $2, $3, '\\ud83c\\udfa4', $4)`,\\n            [`${user_type}: \\\"${raw_transcript.substring(0,30)}\\\"`, `${intent} | ${sentiment}`, user_type, page_route || '/dashboard']\\n        );\\n        \\n        // Pattern\\n        await pool.query(\\n            `INSERT INTO learned_patterns (pattern_name, pattern_text, pattern_type, occurrence_count) VALUES ($1, $2, $3, 1)`,\\n            [raw_transcript.substring(0,50), raw_transcript, intent]\\n        );\\n        \\n        // Update stats\\n        const isBoss = user_type === 'boss' ? 1 : 0;\\n        await pool.query(`\\n            UPDATE learning_stats SET\\n                total_interactions = COALESCE(total_interactions,0) + 1,\\n                ledger_entries = COALESCE(ledger_entries,0) + 1,\\n                boss_inputs = COALESCE(boss_inputs,0) + $1,\\n                patterns_learned = COALESCE(patterns_learned,0) + 1,\\n                tts_responses_given = COALESCE(tts_responses_given,0) + 1,\\n                updated_at = NOW()\\n            WHERE stat_date = CURRENT_DATE\\n        `, [isBoss]);\\n        \\n        console.log(`[OK] Logged and stats updated`);\\n        \\n        res.json({\\n            success: true,\\n            ledger_id: ledger.rows[0].id,\\n            analysis: { sentiment, emotion: {\\n        console.error(`[ERROR] ${err.message}`);\\n        res.status(500).json({ error: err.message });\\n    }\\n});\\n\\n// d.slice(0, 8).map(c => \n                    `<div class=\"item\"><div class=\"item-title\">${c.command_text}</div><div class=\"item-meta\">${c.times_used || 0}x \u2022 ${Math.round((c.success_rate || 0) * 100)}%</div></div>`\n                ).join('') : '<div class=\"item\"><div class=\"item-meta\">No commands yet</div></div>';\n            } catch (e) { console.error('Commands:', e); }\n        }\n        \n        async function loadEmpathy() {\n            try {\n                const r = await fetch(API + '/empathy-patterns');\n                const d = await r.json();\n                document.getElementById('empathyCount').textContent = d.length;\n                document.getElementById('empathy').innerHTML = d.length ? d.slice(0, 8).map(e => \n                    `<div class=\"item\"><div class=\"item-title\" style=\"color:#10b981\">${e.emotion_detected}</div><div class=\"item-meta\">${e.times_used || 0}x \u2022 ${Math.round((e.effectiveness_score || 0) * 100)}%</div></div>`\n                ).join('') : '<div class=\"item\"><div class=\"item-meta\">No empathy data</div></div>';\n            } catch (e) { console.error('Empathy:', e); }\n        }\n        \n        async function loadBossInputs() {\n            try {\n                const r = await fetch(API + '/boss-inputs');\n                const d = await r.json();\n                document.getElementById('bossCount').textContent = d.length;\n                \n                // Check for new items\n                const newId = d[0]?.id || 0;\n                const isNew = newId > lastBossId;\n                lastBossId = newId;\n                \n                document.getElementById('bossInputs').innerHTML = d.length ? }\n        }\n        \n        function loadAll() {\n            loadDash();\n            loadFeed();\n            loadCrawled();\n            loadPatterns();\n            loadCommands();\n            loadEmpathy();\n            loadBossInputs();\n        }\n        \n        loadAll();\n        setInterval(loadAll, 1500);
